// ignore this error:
//   [$rootScope:inprog] $apply already in progress \
//   http://errors.angularjs.org/1.5.9/$rootScope/inprog?p0=%24apply
// these are non-fatal, they are not ideal, but they are noisey
var RX_ROOT_SCOPE_INPROG_ERR = /^\[\$rootScope:inprog\]/
function isRootScopeError (payload) {
  return (
    payload &&
    payload.body &&
    payload.body.trace &&
    payload.body.trace.message &&
    RX_ROOT_SCOPE_INPROG_ERR.test(payload.body.trace.message)
  )
}

// djhaveri 2017-08-18
// ignore angular status: -1 errors
// these happen because of client-side issues for example:
//    * net::ERR_BLOCKED_BY_CLIENT
//    * net::ERR_NETWORK_CHANGED
function isStatusMinus1Error (payload) {
  if (payload && payload.body && payload.body.message && payload.body.message.body) {
    try {
      const body = JSON.parse(payload.body.message.body)
      if (body.status === -1) {
        return true
      }
    } catch (e) { return false }
  }
}

function isIe10 () {
  if (window.navigator.userAgent && window.navigator.userAgent.indexOf('MSIE 10.0') !== -1) {
    return true
  } else {
    return false
  }
}

var _rollbarConfig = {
  accessToken: '492cf5b0690647a095e8596633ef919a',
  captureUncaught: false,
  reportLevel: "warning",
  itemsPerMinute: 3,
  autoInstrument: {
    network: false,
    log: true,
    dom: true,
    navigation: true,
    connectivity: true
  },
  payload: {
    environment: 'production',
    client: {
      javascript: {
        source_map_enabled: true,
        code_version: "3d0e7c4ad9e23fa60ee1980ff3a9dc6dddf426e1",
        guess_uncaught_frames: true
      }
    }
  },
  // return `true` in this function to ignore errors
  checkIgnore: function (isUncaught, args, payload) {
    if (isIe10()) return true
    if (isRootScopeError(payload)) return true
    if (isStatusMinus1Error(payload)) return true
    return false
  }
};
